The `number of followers` of users in Ethiopia on `2023/3/28 12:22 PM UTC`. This list contains users from `Ethiopia` and cities `Addis-ababa` `Dire-dawa` `Dire-dawa` `Hawassa` `Dessie`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/Zaid-maker/top-github-users-list).

There are `990 users`  in Ethiopia. You need at least `4 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
